326 \textcolor{comment}{/*                             TO LIE. INITIALLY .2, ENLARGED TO 1.0 AS */}
327 \textcolor{comment}{/*                             ITERATION COUNT INCREASES. */}
328 \textcolor{comment}{/*                   SAVETA(3) SAVES TOOL AXIS DURING NOTAN STEP. */}
329 \textcolor{comment}{/*                   SAVETE(3) SAVES TOOL END POSITION DURING NOTAN STEP. */}
330 \textcolor{comment}{/*                   SAVES     SAVES DISTANCE TO ALL 3 SURFACES ON ENTRY */}
331 \textcolor{comment}{/*                             TO NOTAN STEP.  USED AS A CRITERION FOR */}
332 \textcolor{comment}{/*                             POSSIBLE RESTART FROM ENTRY TO NOTAN. */}
333 \textcolor{comment}{/*                   SMOVE     MAGNITUDE OF SMALLEST VECTOR WHICH CAN BE */}
334 \textcolor{comment}{/*                             ADDED TO TOOL END WITHIN SINGLE PRECISION. */}
335 \textcolor{comment}{/*                             SET ON ENTRY TO CENTR.   ALL MOVE VECTORS */}
336 \textcolor{comment}{/*                             ARE ENLARGED TO THIS SIZE IF NECESSARY */}
337 \textcolor{comment}{/*                   TANANG    CRITERION FOR ESTABLISHING PSEUDO-TANGENCY */}
338 \textcolor{comment}{/*                             IS DOT(CHECK SURF NORMAL, OTHER SURF */}
339 \textcolor{comment}{/*                             NORMAL) .GT. TANANG.  SET AT 1-.5*TAU. */}
340 
341 \textcolor{comment}{/*                   PURPOSE   TO ITERATE CUTTER TO DESIRED POSITION */}
342 \textcolor{comment}{/*                             RELATIVE TO 2 OR 3 SURFACES */}
